<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>ITEM 7.01. REGULATION FD DISCLOSURE</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">On April 9, 2013, John Brown, the Chief Executive Officer of
Zion Oil &amp; Gas, Inc. (the &quot;Company&quot;) sent an informative letter regarding the Company&rsquo;s new Direct Stock Purchase
Plan to its Company's shareholders and other persons listed on the Company&rsquo;s database addressing recent investment opportunities.
A copy of such letter is attached to this report as Exhibit 99.1.</P>

    <TD STYLE="padding-right: 5.4pt; padding-left: 5.4pt">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding-right: 5.4pt; padding-left: 5.4pt; text-align: justify; padding-top: 3pt"><FONT STYLE="color: black">The&nbsp;<B>Direct Stock Purchase Plan</B>&nbsp;is intended to be a convenient and simple way for you to purchase Zion stock directly from the company, allowing you to build your long-term investment over time while avoiding those dreadful brokerage fees.<BR>
<BR>
The minimum investment is $250.00. Once you have your account set up with our Plan Agent, the Registrar and Transfer Company, you may invest as little as $50.00 at a time. There is also an option for automatic monthly withdrawal directly from your bank account.<BR>
________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________<BR>
<BR>
As mentioned, for a limited time only, you can purchase&nbsp;Units&nbsp;directly through the&nbsp;<B>Direct Stock Purchase Plan</B>. A&nbsp;<B>Unit</B>&nbsp;is comprised of one share of&nbsp;<B>Common Stock</B>&nbsp;and one&nbsp;<B>Warrant</B>&nbsp;and is currently being sold for $2.50 each. The Unit Offering&nbsp;will only be available through August 30, 2013.</FONT></TD></TR>
<TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
    <TD STYLE="padding-right: 5.4pt; padding-left: 5.4pt; color: blue; text-decoration: none">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding-right: 5.4pt; padding-left: 5.4pt">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding-right: 5.4pt; padding-left: 5.4pt; text-align: justify; padding-top: 3pt">&nbsp;</TD></TR>
<TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
    <TD STYLE="padding-right: 5.4pt; padding-left: 5.4pt; color: blue">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding-right: 5.4pt; padding-left: 5.4pt">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 3pt 5.4pt; text-align: justify; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-top: Black 1pt solid">A&nbsp;<B>Warrant</B>&nbsp;is an option to purchase stock&nbsp;for a set price over a set period of time.</TD></TR>
<TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
    <TD STYLE="padding-right: 5.4pt; padding-left: 5.4pt; color: blue; text-decoration: none"><IMG SRC="image_015.jpg" ALT="Description: earn about Units &amp; Warrants" STYLE="height: 174px; width: 214px"></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding-right: 5.4pt; padding-left: 5.4pt">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding-right: 5.4pt; padding-left: 5.4pt; text-align: left; vertical-align: top; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; padding-top: 5pt">If
    you purchase&nbsp;<B>Units</B>&nbsp;through the&nbsp;<B>Direct Stock Purchase Plan</B>, you will get&nbsp;one share of <B>Common
    Stock</B>&nbsp;and&nbsp;one&nbsp;<B>Warrant</B>&nbsp;to purchase one share of&nbsp;<B>Common Stock</B>&nbsp;for a set price
    of $2.00. The Warrant is good for five years. You can exercise your Warrants from September 30, 2013 through September 30,
    2018.<BR>
